 shahrukh khan, ambani or unke samooh ko lekar uda nijee vimaan manahaton se 53 kilometre ke faasale par sthit white plance hawaii adde par dopaher baad paune ek baje utraa
 Sources said that everyone else was immediately given immigration clearance, but Shahrukh was stopped and had to wait till two and a half
 tippaniyan According to sources, the White Plains airport is small and until Shah Rukh got the immigration clearance, everyone else in the group waited for him
 shahrukh ko is tarah roke jane se vah or unke dal ke anya log khaase pareshaan ho gaye or samasya sulajhane kii jaddojahad main jute rahe
 The press conference lasted twenty minutes and during this time Shah Rukh did not say anything about stopping him
 unke dal ke sadasyon or vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon ne bhi unhen roke jane ke kaarnon ke bare main kuch nahin kaha
 When contacted, Shah Rukh said through a member of his team that he would not comment on the episode
 sadsy ne kaha ki shahrukh kaa yah kahana ki america ke avrajan adhikari unki hekdi nikaal dete hai is baat kaa subut he ki unhen is saare vaake se bahut dukh hua he
 Sources said the 46-year-old actor was scheduled to address a press conference at 2 pm and was scheduled to deliver lectures at Yale University at 4 pm although he arrived three hours late from the scheduled time for the press conference and his one-hour run The lecture also started around 6 pm
 vishvavidhyalay main chaatro ko sambodhit karte hue shahrukh ne kaha, ‘‘ jab bhi mujhe khud par gumaan hone lagata he to main america kaa ek chakkar laga letaa hum
 The immigration officers here take out all my arrogance
 ’’ shahrukh ne kaha ki is tarah ke halaat main bhi unke paas unki choti-choti safaltaaon kaa khajaana he
 Shahrukh said, "he (immigration officer) always asks me how tall i am and i always lie that my height is five feet ten inches
" agali baar main thodaa or dussahsee hone vaala hum
 (if he would ask me) What color am I, then i will say blond
 ’’ Sources said that before it was revealed that Shah Rukh had been detained at New York's White Plains Airport, Yale University officials contacted officials from the US Department of Immigration and Customs and Internal Security in Washington
 
 unhone bataaya ki shahrukh khan is puure prakaran se bahut pareshaan the or vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon ko unhen saamaanya karne main lanbaa vakt laga
 Shahrukh has returned to India
 unhen conacticat yel vishvavidhyalay ne apni pratishthit chab faillowship pradaan kii
 As part of the fellowship, Khan addressed hundreds of university students, their parents, faculty and other members of the indo-american community on the Yale campus
 apana sambodhan shuru karne se pehle khan ne kaha ki unki udaan kaaphi lambii thi or vah america laane ke liye ambani ke shukraguzaar hai
 Ambani's daughter Isha studies at Yale University and is also the president of the university's South Asian Society
 khan ne kaha ki unhen ‘‘hameshaa kii tarah hawaii adde par roak liya gaya
 "when the people who came to hear Shah Rukh's address came to know that they were once again stopped at the airport, they were very surprised and they whipped the American authorities, but this most oblivious Indian actor said," It was good as it always is
 ’’ shahrukh ne chaatro ko yahi bataaya ki unhen dedh ghante tak roka gaya haalanki sutron kaa kahana he tha ki unhen do ghante se zyada samay tak hawaii adde par roka gaya
 According to sources, Shah Rukh said that this is not the first time he has been detained at an airport in the US and has been with him three to four times before
 is tarah kaa aakhri vakya 2009 main pesh aayaa tha, jab shahrukh ko neujersey main nevark hawaii adde par roak liya gaya tha

 tippaniyan According to sources, the White Plains airport is small and until Shah Rukh got the immigration clearance, everyone else in the group waited for him

 The press conference lasted twenty minutes and during this time Shah Rukh did not say anything about stopping him
 unke dal ke sadasyon or vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon ne bhi unhen roke jane ke kaarnon ke bare main kuch nahin kaha
 When contacted, Shah Rukh said through a member of his team that he would not comment on the episode
 sadsy ne kaha ki shahrukh kaa yah kahana ki america ke avrajan adhikari unki hekdi nikaal dete hai is baat kaa subut he ki unhen is saare vaake se bahut dukh hua he
 Addressing the students at the university, Shah Rukh said, "whenever i feel proud of myself, i take a round of America
 yahaan ke avrajan adhikari meri sari hekdi nikaal dete hai
 Shahrukh said that even under such circumstances, he has a wealth of his small successes
 shahrukh ne kaha, ‘‘ vah (avrajan adhikari) hameshaa mujhase poochhate hai ki meraa kad kitna he or main hameshaa jhooth bolta hum ki meraa kad paanch foot das inch he
 Next time I'm going to be a little more adventurous
 (agar vah mujhase puuchhenge) meraa rang kya he to main kah duungaa gora
 '' sutron ne bataaya ki isse purv jab yah maaloom hua ki shahrukh ko neuyork ke white plance hawaii adde par roak liya gaya he to yel vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon ne washington sthit america avrajan or seemaa shulk vibhaag or aantarik suraksha vibhaag ke adhikariyon se is bare main sampark kiya
 He told that Shah Rukh Khan was very upset with this whole episode and it took the university authorities a long time to normalize him
 shahrukh bharat waapas laut aae hai
 He was awarded his prestigious Chubb Fellowship by the Connecticut Yale University
 faillowship ke antargat khan ne vishvavidhyalay ke saikadon chaatro, unke abhibhavako, faikalti or bharat america samudaay ke anya sadasyon ko yel parisar main sambodhit kiya
 Before starting his address, Khan said that his flight was very long and he was thankful to Ambani for bringing him to America
 ambani kii putree isha yel vishvavidhyalay main padhati he or vishvavidhyalay ke dakshin asian samaaj kii adhyaksh bhi he
 Khan said he was "detained" at the airport as usual
 ’’ shahrukh kaa sambodhan sunne aae logon ko jab yah maaloom hua ki unhen ek baar phir hawaii adde par roak liya gaya tha to vah log khaase hairaan hue or unhone america adhikariyon ko jeebhar kosa, lekin is sabase bekhbar bhartiya abhinayta ne kaha, ‘‘yah acha tha kyonki yah hameshaa hota he
 Shah Rukh told the students that he was detained for one and a half hours, although sources said that he was detained at the airport for more than two hours
 sutron ke anusaar shahrukh ne kaha ki yah pehla mauka nahin he, jab unhen america main hawaii adde par roka gaya he or isse pehle bhi teen se chaar baar unke saath aisa ho chukaa he
 The last such incident occurred in 2009, when Shah Rukh was detained at Newark Airport in New Jersey
 shahrukh kaa kahana tha uske naam ke saath chunki khan judaa he isliye unhen nevark antararashtriya hawaii adde par kareeb do ghante ke liye roak liya gaya tha
 The private plane carrying Shah Rukh Khan, Ambani and his group landed at White Plains Airport, 53 kilometers from Manhattan, at 1:30 pm
 sutron ne bataaya ki baaki sab ko to turant avrajan manjuuri de di gai, lekin shahrukh ko roak liya gaya or unhen dhai baje tak intjaar karnaa padaa
 The comments sutron ke anusaar white plance hawaii adda chota-sa he or jab tak shahrukh ko avrajan manjuuri nahin mil gai, samooh ke baaki sabhi log unka intjaar karte rahe
 Stopping Shah Rukh in this way, he and others of his party were greatly disturbed and were struggling to solve the problem
 samvaadadaata sammelan bees minute chalaa or is dauraan shahrukh ne unhen roke jane ke bare main kuch nahin kaha
 His team members and university officials also did not say anything about the reasons for his detention
 is bare main sampark kiye jane par shahrukh ne apane dal ke ek sadsy kii marfat kaha ki is prakaran par vah koi tippanee nahin karenge
 The member said that Shah Rukh's assertion that the US immigration officials expel his arrogance is a proof that he is deeply saddened by this incident
